### Engine Types

	tank_gasoline_engine = {
		abbreviation = "gas"
		category = tank_engine_type
		sfx = sfx_ui_sd_module_engine

		add_stats = {
			build_cost_ic = 3
			fuel_consumption = 2
			maximum_speed = 1
		}
		multiply_stats = {
			maximum_speed = 0.15
		}

	}

		}
